et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And when we assist, if we heat the fine cautery according to the size of the fistula, as was previously mentioned;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	And pour heat throughout the fistula until it comes from under the foundation; and perform this twice or three times, as long as you know that these charred parts are burnt, which resemble a feather of a bird.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then treat the wet cloths with butter until that burnt part comes out, then apply ointment to adhere to the burn and bond it together.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it is done this way, it is right. If not, nothing else can be done in this manner.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it is prodded through, and does not pierce until the point which is or serves as a foundation, and in between your finger and the tent there's a thick layer of flesh or silk, and you can see the fistula at that place where the layer meets the skin;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if it's during the beginning of the fistula formation, and it stays before the tent, then after that apply the cautery until it reaches the tip of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	the tent will be removed and it will drain. Then remove those thorns that look like a bird's feather, and don't leave any behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if it doesn't heal with the skin, cut between you and the wound, then apply either fire or an ague medicine cautery.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For the fire cautery brings together two important things: this is to say, the blistering of these heated rods, and the bleeding of blood and the evaporation of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the application of greasy cloths or ground things to wet areas, until his limbs stop bleeding, and the heated rods burn within the wound;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with hot, sticking bandages, and use dry medicinal substances.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, if it is healed and does not recur.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes just up to half of its depth, and is far from the body, seal it with your hand or the base, and inquire about this.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	And if you feel the tentacle, and it's halfway between two threads or a string or needles, or it's almost about to pierce, but there is only a channel of needlework and hope outside, through the application of one of three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it down to the base, or if you can, use a tentacle and cure as the first step;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and don't go too deep down below, that you might cut the support of the base, and allow the discharges to pass voluntarily through it;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then the treatment, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance if it is clean, or you remove that covering and wash it since it has been cut from under the root, either by probing or with another tool directed;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then cleanse that which is sown in the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then strive to heal the wound and keep the pus within the lower part of the root: if it is easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And it is not done in this manner for any holes: and when you press the tent into the hole, and she is at the spot where the bottom lies beneath the skin above,
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	take a tent pierced through the head according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And tie two twisted threads together, and press the tent into the hole until it reaches the head along the entire length of the thread.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is deep in the fold beneath the bottom, then remove that twisted thread as long as you hold your finger on the bottom;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	And pull the head through the thread, and join together the two shoulders as one, and hold one to the other, and leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	And hold them repeatedly until the threads have gone through these parts that are between the two shoulders, and unite them;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	Then treat the wound until it is healed and has recovered.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open, make an incision in all possible ways until it opens, as long as it is not too close to perfection.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not suitable to do this procedure of placing a splint correctly first and then treat, as we have said, until it heals.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spinous puncture that one makes for the fistula is small and from one side and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand no, because what should not be done should not be done either, as you see here:
des emorroydes	from bloodletting
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Excoriations occur in two ways: or they are within the foundation, like a piece of resin, and if there are small and large ones, bleeding ensues.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and when there is one or more of them, they are found either outside the foundation and near its base; but those that are outside have little moisture.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	and often when there is a bit of lemon water or a trace of blood, they have the color of the skin.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	The treatment for those who have them within the foundation consists in commanding the patient to spread out under cover until the foundations pass through and you can see the threads.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you are swift, grip it with pincers, or hold it by your finger nail, then cut into its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the limb cannot be held due to its moisture, take it by halves, or with cloth, or from a camel hair fabric;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And extract them with your fingers, then cut them, and dust them with some hot powders that are used for cauterization.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you can sear them as it is said or according to the chapter on cauterization, and then continue with other treatments until they heal.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the foundations cannot escape, instruct the patient to apply a blistering agent that burns and is harsh to wash away what lies under or in the foundations, so that it might escape freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	And if the body parts cannot proceed, and if the threads are too strong at the foundation, then the treatment should be gentle;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you should take them with your fingernail or tweezers, and pull them out, then treat them as we have said, until it is healed, and fears the iron incision.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	It is necessary that you sew it in this manner: take one twisted thread, and put it on a needle, then pull the thread over and pierce the needle from another side, and twist both ends of the thread around the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	And if it be large; and keep the thread in form, then tie the thread, and pull out the needle, and do so with all others, and leave one for bleeding off the excess of blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	And then place one moistened pad in oil rose or as a poultice, and place it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then leave it until the pus drains out, and when they have settled, treat with ointment and other treatments, until he is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	By drying through the fire or the foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times, there is severe bleeding in the intestines, due to nature's compulsion and when the illness has become old and medicine no longer provides benefit.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you reset at the tip of a thorn or on your nail, which should not be left in moisture.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it while it is hard as it should be;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot harden, redo the shaving with more force than before, until some flesh is cleaned off and it is properly scorched;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him as long as he remains healthy.
dou fremit	with trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Ants is a small false appearance beneath the body, and they move about within it;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And at no time does the real vein cool down, and one feels it also like death by trembling, spreading throughout the body, and more in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a piece of goose feather or a strong vulture feather and place that stick over the twitching spot, until the purple circle encompasses the twitching completely.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand until you grip all the stick as long as you cover completely the twitching area, and place it downward, and pull out the twitching from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see fit, make it in the form of a reed or iron stick like this, and ensure it is thin going under and thick coming up.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not make it too thin; you must hold onto both ends and squeeze it. If you can see, use the cautery to cauterize the twitching as shown or described in the section about fire cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	From the shape of the bladder
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Never make a bladder out of silver or archaut, or molten iron or maillechet; and never make these small and large tools according to their intended use.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	So therefore, when dealing with the treatment of children and those who are weak and painful, they should be small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the bladder, whether small or large, is thus above broad; or the stomachs are bound in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	And there is a condition where the belly and intestines are intertwined, as you see, and the head goes inside; and has two holes on one side, and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	And there is where the belly or where we insert medications from a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with tiny holes.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And there is between each hole exactly one finger's width of space, then insert into these holes two threads made from spun cloth, twisted for ten or twelve turns around each other, and attach the belly as if it were a goat.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And when the medicine is inside, tie it with a strong thread in front of the tool, then seal it; and this forms like a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and smear the head with oil or yolk of egg ointment, or similar thing, then gently apply it.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then spread the ministers with both hands combined, as long as you can see clearly, then extract the lump, and lift the patient's legs up to show.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if the medicine seems to be going out, let it escape as much as possible; and if they sleep for a whole night, that is more help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you use it in the disease of stomach passage and the medicine starts to escape quickly, redo it as long as it is safe.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if they leak from their root or from an abscess, even if the bladder is so fine as through a child's finger;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and it's the form of a subtle bladder above which the skin is restricted:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have spoken about the treatment of wounds in our division; now we will discuss hand surgery and medicine according to completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I state that wounds are varied according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and for why they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The reasons wounds are made are through impact from stone, size of sword and knife cuts, or from spear, staff, or axe strikes, or through similar actions.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or depending on the parts of the body, such as a wound made on the neck or head, or chest, or stomach, or liver, and similar limbs.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and start with simple head injuries, because memory will recall it in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound appears or the head comes out, and if the bone is not broken, take care to determine whether it's due to stone or similar things, and the skin has been torn completely and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you doubt slightly about the abscess: if it is done promptly with the surgeon's knife even if there is a little blood from the wound, and so the surgery goes against the severed part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and let the patient drink plenty of wine and eat rich meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to be operated on, then reduce his meat intake, and do not drink wine, nor eat any kind of meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And when it comes to a wound, if pus appears there, use wet cotton dipped in rose oil or in a tincture of wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if no pus is present, then apply to the wound, if it is fresh with all its blood and not disturbed by the air, a powder that I will mention shortly;
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it has been burned, then apply some ointments until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like that of a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be stitched together with bandages, then stitch them together, as I will explain for wounds on the belly, by stitching.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is revealed by bone and muscle, and it only holds for a little bit if you press; then treat the wound with medicine, and restore hard tissue instead of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	And instruct the patient to eat large meats, such as kidneys and cooked wheat, also like chickens or similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find that the skin has turned to rot and it doesn't smell like bone, if the rot has reached all over, let it completely decompose and release its odor, then treat it;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if an artery is located in the wound or vein, without a cut, and it cannot be stopped by medicine, if you find the artery bleeding, cut it, and if you discover that it has ruptured, sew it up with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if this does not benefit you, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, treat them with a light cure: and you should put on this powder which seals in such a way that when the heat has passed, it stays firmly.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the way to make this powder is as follows: take part of incense; dragon's blood one and a half parts; live charcoal three parts, and finely powdered,
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	And tend to the wound, and keep it bandaged, until it properly drains and fully joins its own blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And apply it well, and let it heal naturally without bursting; for one does not remove the medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And one performs this only with salt alone, when one does not have the incense or the blood of dragon, but when the medicine has healed the wound.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the medicine has healed the wound, even then, do not put this powder in it;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	But apply on some poultices that have been digested, or oats flour made with water and honey, as long as it oozes bile;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then perform other treatments as long as they are sound.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the breaking of bones comes with the wound and it is small, then extract them with delicate tweezers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about the fractures of the head later.
de la plaie dou col	From the wound of the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	That wound comes from the neck and it is simple; if there's no distinction between one and another in the neck or around the throat, but when the neck veins or the artery are cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it's the nerves, then there is no other means than to leave the treatment, and not to put any restraining thing, because it harms the nerves and causes them to recede;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not place anything cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and that continues with it so they are connected to the brain, which is the highest member;
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but if the medicine is liquid, such as when it's washed with mild water and mixed with rose oil, and also washed lettuce in mild water too,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other minerals in this manner, and wet applications.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, one sews and binds it with bandages, then treats it as long as it heals properly.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and filled with blood, one punctures them or deeper,
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is severed and blood starts flowing out, one must open it, heal it, and cauterize it;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the throat or ribs are severed, or the passage is kept intact through which meat goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if you burn on the base of the throat, and do not touch the throat but instead adjust it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then tighten the dressing, and leave it for some days, then treat with dried dressings until it heals;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if there is an appearance of bone in the wound, then take care of that;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are fragments of bone, remove them all if you can, and leave those that you cannot obtain until the wound heals;
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And when freed and cured of its trouble;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, apply the powder that I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has an opening, treat it as instructed in this chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	Regarding the wound from a spear or a knife.
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it's a wound from a lance or knife, and the injury is deep, when you look inside the wound to see if there is an obstruction: know then that the wound is fatal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it's not deep and is full of blood at all times inside when fresh, should you not apply the powder right away in the first hour or tie it up because the blood won't clot properly from lack thereof.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and warm him to his heart, and occupy the patient;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment, and bandage it twice a day.;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	And if you don't have anointment, put old cotton into the wound to suck out the moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and make the patient rest on the wound for 3 days, or 4, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no convulsions occur, nor harmful trembling of the heart, nor sudden movements;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see good signs, you know that the wound has been saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat then with other remedies until the blood is clear;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot be cleared and operated on, know that there is a fistula; treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife cut, and it's simple, or worse, or on the back, treat it according to the person in front.
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	And if it's large, sew it up; and if it's small, use powder; and if it's deep into the bone or has torn through it, clean the wound and remove any foreign objects inside.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not cleaned, leave the wound to fester, letting ease the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And about other wounds on other limbs is the judgement similarly as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	From the rupture of the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The ruptures of the belly are large, medium-sized, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	In a large wound, once the intestines or the ends of the intestines are exposed, due to their intrusion;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And the stitches are more difficult, and nothing beats the small wound over the large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	for this reason one cannot insert the intestines again easily, unless they are done so step by step;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell almost immediately when they sense coldness, it is no longer possible to insert them again.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And for this reason, we let the animal's wound heal, because in doing so, we move the intestines back to their place where they should be.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	Know that the rupture of the belly occurs in four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common stitches happen at the abdominal seam,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the other stitches related to injuries in the body and two more specific stitches for other injuries are commonly used with other injuries;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And still they are more proper with the suture of the belly, and I will say each one and explain them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing of the intestine sticks out,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And when it comes to binding up such a thing, this can be done in two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	Or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	Because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when he is cold, warm him up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	Moisten a sponge or use one part of molten wax dipped solely in water.
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	Or cook in water containing lime and thyme, and spikes,
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And let the intestine grow until the belly button is removed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And after this has been done with the wine strainers, and once it has been made muddy for the purpose of reducing swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see that the swelling is leaving, then moisten the intestine with water or with broth that has been cooked well.
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	because through this, the entry accepts little of what comes in;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, they make a little opening at the tool with which one removes the hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	And the first treatment is to have the wound dried after being cut,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	That we should not cut it without great necessity or if there's no need;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And this is the tool to split it:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	If you cut within the bend or outside, see this shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged and the intestines leap out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if you place it back according to its natural shape in its proper location,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you can, because this moves them.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is broad, and it's located on the lower part of the abdomen,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	It is necessary that you allow the patient to lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and place his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it's located in the lower abdomen area,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	Put the head and buttocks higher than the parts below,
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	And also if there is a rupture in the belly near one of the two parts,
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	and make sure that the part which was dragged goes higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and thus, it is to follow what I say in great and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	Treating small wounds requires you to provide what suits them,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then hold between your hands...I. minister remedies that heal the entire wound with her hand,
et assemble les levres;	and bring the lips together;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	And this is the common method of sewing,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	And you should take one or more needles, according to the size of the wound's width,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	Then leave at the edge of the wound two inches, and insert one needle where there is half an inch of thick strong thread;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce the two edges of the skin with the two needles from the thimble,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is under the skin, as long as you pierce it from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and join the two chief points of siphacing the three together;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then tighten with a doubled thread around the needle for half a turn,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	and join the two edges of the wound together.
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	And then leave one inch of space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then weave the thread like you did with the first needle.
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue doing this according to your skill with needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound is treated;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	And use needles of medium size, between fine and thick ones,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because the thin needles cut all the flesh, and the very thick ones cannot enter at all well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	for this is why they should be of medium size;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not good to have the needles sticking out too far from the flesh and the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	Let them not cut and open the wound before suturing;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then pull out the needles, so they do not irritate the patient at night,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and cover the needle holes with bandages or cloths to keep them clean,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound is stitched closed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	And this method of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	for it takes one needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second type of stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And it consists in sewing together two parts of leather and two parts of sinew with one needle, using thread that is half as thick as the material being sewn.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	And when you have pierced these joints all four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	then pull the needle to the part where you started piercing, in the manner one sews threads;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and leave a space between each stitch as large as half a doigtm.
ceste costure sevent li home,	these stitches form the bandage,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	And here I treat a wound where someone had or stomach,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	who was pierced by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound was larger than a palm in size,

et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	And the wound healed up to fifteen days, I treated it, and it became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	And I would not cure with ointment, for I was at one place where none could be found or no remedies;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And I would put cotton twice a day over the wound, and wash it in honey water until it was clean.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper ways of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle, and insert it from the outer part up to that inner side;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When she has pierced through the vein straight on, if it is at the neck or under the armpit where you have stuck the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	and makes her pierce from another side through the inner part until she reaches that spot below.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	And as for sewing this seam, it's like how the tailor sews skins, so you should sew it in the same way.
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And leave one thread on one side, and then take another from the other, until you finish sewing all the seam.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of suture, as Galen stated precisely,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	If it's like what others do, bringing together the two parts naturally,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and press one end of the needle to the other, like this:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	stitch a needle or the end of the thread near the eyebrow, and only pierce that one.
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	and let the two shoulders grow smooth;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	then turn the needle and make it pierce from the outer part down to the inner side,
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	like the two shoulders smoothly;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce both from the outer part down to the inner side, like two other smooth shoulders on the opposite side;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the usual method of suturing and the most common way.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen spoke these words, and none would testify to them,
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One must stitch the belly with two needles, or if there is thread in each;
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	And one should sew one needle from one side and the other from the other, like those who stitch coins.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when there's rupture within the belly,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	then the stitches are more painful than in other parts of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments for this wound are like those for other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it's as follows when you find the fresh wound with all its blood, just as the art has made it.
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	If you reposition it within the intestine, and then stitch; afterwards place the invigorating powder.

puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as usual until it heals;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you don't have medicine, place it there, as soon as it begins to bleed, old cotton.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it twice a day until it heals.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you don't need any other medicines in various preparations when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt that the wound might affect the main members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	If it is necessary for you to moisten with a light oil of a warmed substance, or in an oil roasting heat,

Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine referred to as 'juvenile' cannot be healed when it is poisoned,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And that's due to the location of the veins there and because of the subtlety of the entire body, and its closeness to the nature of the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the knot jumps out of the wound, then reset it back in the same way as the intestine when it is fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it has become old and turned brown or black, then you should tie the black area, so that no blood flows there.

de la routure dou boueil	Of the rupture of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestine is torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	if it can be restored in any way,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen that some were pierced in the belly by a lance;

Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	Those who heat up inside their intestines, and cause no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	And one can tie the intestine with a fine thread that has been cut from an animal's intestine,

pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take hold of this cut intestine thread, so that most of it is raw,
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	And then at the head of this thread .1. linen thread fine twined,
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then sew the thread in the needle, and stitch the intestine, then reset it at the incision;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this way of sewing is not far off as long as it follows the path of love and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and broad, especially when it's in one of the parts of the intestine, if there's no obstruction or sickness, then use subtle technique.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of a sinus or if it be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, when it matures, is universally called "sinus".
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And similarly when it's sealed and starts to heal.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	A sinus is according to the truth of the hard swelling that is white and firm, where no pain is felt,
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and is also as hairy as the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	and sometimes it is clear and thin, and other times thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	sometimes insufficient, and other times enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	and I have discussed this in the section on wounds, that every wound not healed, and there is no pus,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	This happens only through one of the eight reasons:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	It is known as, because of the weakness in blood or pus;
ou por sa malice;	or due to its malevolence;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is tough flesh within and on the lips that doesn't allow new flesh to grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	There is too much blood;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or the lungs are congested, and the matter is of bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine is not good in the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption resembles the plague;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	Due to its location being late in the digestive process, and health becoming slow, it escapes naturally;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	There are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments with medicine in this section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	So it is necessary for me to inform you about the treatment of a fistula which is done by manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistulas occur in all limbs of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that originate from large veins, and arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or at the stomach, or in the intestines, or in the bladder, or in any of the ribs,
