et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and place wet cloths around it, to prevent the patient from getting burnt, then extend each minister towards him, and set their position equal to his hand in case of dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin. Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If it returns, that's good. If not, place him on a table and press him like we have said in the gymnastics, and lie the patient on his healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when the dislocation is in front, it must be extended as soon as possible, and according to what I said; and make the patient feel their pain on the wrong side, then press with the other hand, and extend downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les .ij. hainches;	And if the dislocation is at the back, it does not suit to extend the patient backward or to raise them up from the ground, instead they should be positioned as their hip was previously dislocated towards the back, just like we said about lying on both hips.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	And should be at their face, and the line extended as we said previously, and one must press on the joint from the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	And it will be right when the limbs stretch their legs and they are equal. So adjust the hips, put on the plaster, and strain with a bandage, so that the hip does not move.
et se repose .iij. jors ou .iiij., puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse. iij. jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And let it rest for three or four days, then release and put on the plaster again; and if you see that they are equal, strain in the same manner as before, and leave it like this for another three days; then release and allow it to move completely until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the shoulder joint
Li genous est desaluez selonc .iij. manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The shoulder joint is dislocated in three ways: this means, inside and outside, and behind; and it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs for this are that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at their knee, and if they do not straighten at their knee, know that they are dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all this is that you make the patient sit up straight, and extend their leg if they can, and place your back against their buttocks, and put their foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les .ij. costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	Then take his knee in your hands and pull it between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the knee. And have other assistants extend their legs as far as the knee returns to its place, until you see that the leg is comfortably aligned with the thigh.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort .iij. jors ou iiij., puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then place the dressing on it and have them move their leg from knee to thigh, then hold them together firmly for 1.5 or 2 days, then release them; do not disturb the injured limbs until the body parts are strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the limbs aren't properly set yet, apply strong extension, as we have said in treating the hip, until it heals well.
de la dislocation dou talon	From the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are never fully set and always partially dislocated, both inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and tends forward to the part where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The reduction should be easy; when it is properly set, you should gently extend it with your hands only if it was correctly positioned.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne .i. ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is reset completely, you should have the patient stand straight, and hold them up with two assistants behind by their leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre .ij. fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, and then with your left hand as well four times, then stretch them up high, and firmly hold the foot up.
et fai ce .ij. fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	and do this twice as we have said, while holding and pulling the foot; if it returns, that is good; if not, restart the process because it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche .i. passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return this way, make the patient sit behind their back on the ground, and place a stick firmly in the earth between their buttocks, and tie cloths around them to prevent the patient from being hurt.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a .i. liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then let the surgeons cut the knee, and other surgeons extend his feet or up to two inches, so he ties them around the neck of the foot;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then extend each surgeon equally, and have them place the tools directly between the knees of the patient so they can hold the patient when one extends.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then place the mirrors equally on both sides of the dislocation with your hands, and have other surgeons cut the healthy leg at the knee, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is at the right point, apply the plaster and bind it tightly on top, then firmly tighten everything, and tie the foot to the leg, and watch the nerves that are above the ankle bone, making sure the bandages are not too tight.
puis le laisse .ij. jors ou .iij., et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par .iiij. jors;	Then leave it for two or three days, and if the wound heals up, restrain it; then release it on the third day or the fourth, and direct the patient not to move for four days afterwards;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if he goes beyond this period, it's not safe that he hasn't been dislocated again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the abscesses come out, then it is necessary that you soothe them, as we have said elsewhere, until they are clean.
des dois	do not specify
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both shoulders are dislocated, if they fit beautifully to extend with work, and this is a minor matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus .i. leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in none of the bones of the back or stones, it should be that you make the patient lie on .i. his full length or .ii. the table completely straight, and place your foot on what opens from these joints, then press with your foot firmly until he recovers;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a .ij. chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse .iij. jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when they are even, and there is nothing opening, place under the foot's sole a shoulder table for two shoulders, then press it firmly, and leave him three days, then reset him; and let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	regarding wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When injury occurs with dislocation and one wishes to restore it, many times it happens that the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	If you are not presumptuous in the treatment, if you do not know the art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and merciful but rather slow to act, do not be hasty.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	And start with soothing things for abscesses, and let the patient's body rely on God, if you do not see any hope of improvement in health.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	And when you do see hope, immediately reset the limb at its place, so that the abscesses drain and heal.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	And when limbs are at their place, administer calming remedies for abscesses and cuts, and treat the wound as it should be treated, using dried ointments;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if accompanied by dislocation and fractures of small bones, set the bones, and do as we have instructed in cases of simple illnesses.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors. Amen	And guard against entering paths of fear according to what I have said, for this befits you as per your Creator, and by the wisdom with which you arm yourself and care for your body. Amen.
Explicit le romen de fisique	End of the physical description.
